beginSubroutine: s32'Afro_MeshSetCheck'
  ifNot: Mem(Afro)
    ifOperation: (IS_NOT_EQUAL), Mem(Afro), Mem(PlayerVal7)
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal7), Mem(Afro)
      resetDefaultMeshSet: 
      meshSetClearNameExchange: 
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'nohead', s32'nohead'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'headonly', s32'headonly'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'MS_1', s32'MS_1'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'MS_2', s32'MS_2'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei_POT', s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei_POT'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei_FAU', s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei_FAU'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei_SLY', s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei_SLY'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'800cs', s32'800cs'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'500cs', s32'500cs'
      setMeshChangeCurrent: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  else: 
    ifOperation: (IS_NOT_EQUAL), Mem(Afro), Mem(PlayerVal7)
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal7), Mem(Afro)
      setDefaultMeshSet: s32'Nohood'
      meshSetClearNameExchange: 
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'nohead', s32'nohead_Nohood'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'headonly', s32'headonly_Nohood'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'MS_1', s32'MS_1_Nohood'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'MS_2', s32'MS_2_Nohood'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei_POT', s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei_POT_N'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei_FAU', s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei_FAU_N'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei_SLY', s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei_SLY_N'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'800cs', s32'800cs_Nofood'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'500cs', s32'500cs_Nofood'
      setMeshChangeCurrent: 
    endIf: 
  endElse: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei'
  ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'pot'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    debugLogForScript: s32'pot', 0, 0
  endIf: 
  ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'fau'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(2)
      debugLogForScript: s32'113', 0, 0
      createObject: s32'Fau500cs', (PLAYER)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(3)
      debugLogForScript: s32'313', 0, 0
      displayMesh: s32'Fau500cs', 1
    endIf: 
    debugLogForScript: s32'fau', 0, 0
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(0)

          homing: (ACCELERATE_TO_SPEED), (STACK1), (PLAYER), 0, 0, 0, -170000, 0, 36000, 0, 60000

        homing: (ACCELERATE_TO_SPEED), (STACK1), (PLAYER), 0, 0, 0, -170000, 0, 37000, 0, 60000
      endIf:

    if: Mem(Tmp)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg6), Val(1)
      addPositionY: 0, 20000
